) AS s ON c."CouponId" = s."CouponId"

    SELECT c1."CouponUsageId", c1."CouponId", c1."OrderId", c1."UsedAt", o."OrderId" AS "OrderId0", o."AddressId", o."CreatedAt", o."FinalAmount", o."OrderDate", o."OrderNumber", o."OrderStatusId", o."TotalCouponAmount", o."TotalProductAmount", o."TotalShippingAmount", o."UpdatedAt", o."UserId"
